i should mention quinn 's predecessors as illinois governors , george ryan and rod blagojevich .
before becoming governor , ryan had been secretary of state , in charge of ( among other things ) the department of motor vehicles .
in 1994 , a baptist minister from chicago was driving with his wife and their six children .
their van was rear - ended by a semi and the children were killed .
the truck driver had a valid illinois license , but could only speak spanish .
this was odd because the written test to get an illinois truck driver 's license is only given in english .
so how did the man get his license ?
it was quickly discovered that examiners in the dmv were accepting bribes in exchange for giving licenses to unqualified drivers .
what infuriated people was that the dmv examiners were expected to contribute very generously to ryan 's political war chest -- up to 10 % of their salaries .
so they took the bribes largely to make the forced contributions to ryan .
ryan wound up in a federal pen .

you should read before posting because your own link says you are wrong !
from your link : 

 a commonly held misconception concerning the rules of marine navigation is that by following specific rules , a vessel can gain certain rights of way over other vessels .
no vessel ever has absolute " right of way " over other vessels .
rather , there can be a " give way " ( burdened ) vessel and a " stand on " ( privileged ) vessel , or there may be two give way vessels with no stand on vessel .
a stand on vessel does not have an absolute right of way over any give way vessel , for if there is a risk of collision , a stand on vessel may still be obliged under rule 2 and rule 17 to give way so as to avoid it , if doing so will be effective and is practicable .
two power - driven vessels approaching each other head to head , are both deemed to be " give way " and both are required to alter course so as to avoid colliding with the other .
neither vessel has " right of way " .

the upshot of this whole issue is that the state of hawaii , the federal government and the people who live , work and visit here have failed to protect our endangered species .
despite all of the tireless efforts of dedicated staff and volunteers to restore native plants and animal species , there seems to be little " political will " to properly fund and enforce regulations and staffing .
the dlnr has been the stepchild of the state government for years , and its ability to protect native species and historic sites has been severely impaired by political interference and lack of support .

as a native hawaiian myself , i was pleased when keith robinson shared thousands of his seed collections from rare native plants with the public so that these could be grown in people 's back yards .

most of those job losses were inevitable , as south african farmers were forced to become more mechanised and efficient .
the problem was n't farmers becoming more efficient and shedding jobs , though .
the problem was that there were no jobs to absorb the unemployed farm labourers .
perhaps better mechanisms could have been put into place to reduce the job losses , but the fact is that sa agriculture in the 80s over - relied on cheap labour .
a farm with , say , 30 employees in south africa would have employed maybe four or five were it transported to an equivalent environment in australia or the us .
i saw that for myself in scotland , where a 4000 ha farm with five different income streams employed about 8 full - time people , including the farmer and his wife .

this article is in support of " pay equity " being applied to all sectors of the economy .
as many have noted , it is the type of job , some male dominated ( e.g. , miner ) and others female dominated ( e.g. , retails sales clerk ) , that accounts for a significant part of the wage difference .
when the public sector unions attacked this issue , they came up with something they called " pay equity " , which does not mean the same pay for a job , whether performed by a male or a female .
instead , pay equity involves bureaucrats and consultants scoring jobs on a point scale ( a completely arbitrary and unscientific process ) .
if they conclude , as they typically do , that the points for a female - dominated job are the same as the points they assign to a male - dominated job ,   then the pay is the same - a receptionist can be paid the same as an electrician in the public sector .
and salaries can only increase under pay equity - the salary of the receptionist is raised to that of the electrician .

the former minor orders ( porter , exorcist , lector and acolyte ) were reserved to men preparing for priesthood .
they were received subsequent to tonsure , by which the candidate became a cleric .
reclaiming the ancient practice , the liturgical renewal intended to return to lay persons ministries that are proper to them .
the minor orders were suppressed and the ministries of lector and acolyte were established .
the intention was that persons would prepare for these ministries and then be formally and publicly instituted in them .
some dioceses were beginning to plan guidelines for selecting and training candidates .
at the last minute , a directive came from the vatican reserving these ministries to men .
since the ministries are still required steps for candidates for deacon and priest , the directive effectively re - clericalized ministries which are proper to both women and men .
there is no liturgical or theological reason for the directive ; it is rooted in fear .
